leading-[24px]"><p>Whether a PTAN (Provider Transaction Access Number) is required for transaction enrollment.</p>
<p>The Provider Transaction Access Number (PTAN) is a Medicare-issued number given to providers upon enrollment with Medicare. This number is usually six digits and is assigned based on the type of service and the location of the provider. Upon enrollment, Medicare Administrating Contracting (MAC) providers should receive their assigned PTAN number in their approval letter.</p></div></div><div class="text-sm border-t openapi-property <ul>
<li><code>ONE_CLICK</code> indicates that once you submit the transaction enrollment request, Stedi can complete the rest of the enrollment process without any further action from you.</li>
<li><code>MULTI_STEP</code> indicates that you must complete additional steps to finish the enrollment process. Customer support will reach out with clear instructions explaining how to complete any remaining steps.</li>

class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>Whether transaction enrollment is single or multi-step.</p>
<ul>

<li><code>MULTI_STEP</code> indicates that you must complete additional steps to finish the enrollment process. Customer support will reach out with clear instructions explaining how to complete any remaining steps.</li>

<ul>
<li><code>ONE_CLICK</code> indicates that once you submit the transaction enrollment request, Stedi can complete the rest of the enrollment process without any further action from you.</li>
<li><code>MULTI_STEP</code> indicates that you must complete additional steps to finish the enrollment process. Customer support will reach out with clear instructions explaining how to complete any remaining steps.</li>

class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>Whether transaction enrollment is single or multi-step.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>ONE_CLICK</code> indicates that once you submit the transaction enrollment request, Stedi can complete the rest of the enrollment process without any further action from you.</li>
<li><code>MULTI_STEP</code> indicates that you must complete additional steps to finish the enrollment process. Customer support will reach out with clear instructions explaining how to complete any remaining steps.</li>

class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>Whether transaction enrollment is single or multi-step.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>ONE_CLICK</code> indicates that once you submit the transaction enrollment request, Stedi can complete the rest of the enrollment process without any further action from you.</li>
<li><code>MULTI_STEP</code> indicates that you must complete additional steps to finish the enrollment process. Customer support will reach out with clear instructions explaining how to complete any remaining steps.</li>

width="24" height="24" fill="currentColor" class="remixicon size-3.5"><path d="M3 4H21V6H3V4ZM3 19H17V21H3V19ZM3 14H21V16H3V14ZM3 9H17V11H3V9Z"></path></svg>String</span></div></div><div class="prose-no-margin pt-4 pb-4 empty:hidden text-[15px] leading-[24px]"><p>Whether transaction enrollment is single or multi-step.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>ONE_CLICK</code> indicates that once you submit the transaction enrollment request, Stedi can complete the rest of the enrollment process without any further action from you.</li>
<li><code>MULTI_STEP</code> indicates that you must complete additional steps to finish the enrollment process. Customer support will reach out with clear instructions explaining how to complete any remaining steps.</li>
